	padding-bottom:0;

						<div class="fl-post-feed-meta">
				<div class="fl-post-feed-terms">
					<div class="fl-terms-label"><div class='fl-glossary-cat'><span><span class="armament">Armament</span></span><span><span class="brevity">Comm Brevity</span></span></div></div>

	</div>
		</div></div>

<div class="fl-post-grid-post fl-post-align-default post-5272 glossary type-glossary status-publish hentry sort_alphabetical-a glossary-cat-armament wpbf-post" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/CreativeWork">
	<meta itemscope itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage" itemid="https://www.fighterpilotpodcast.com/glossary/aargm/" content="AARGM" /><meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-07-02" /><meta itemprop="dateModified" content="2020-01-24" /><div itemprop="publisher" itemscope itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization"><meta itemprop="name" content="The Fighter Pilot Podcast"><div itemprop="logo" itemscope itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject"><meta itemprop="url" content="https://www.fighterpilotpodcast.com/wp-content/uploads/FPP-Logo-Rgb-Photo-Trademark.png"></div></div><div itemscope itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person"><meta itemprop="url" content="https://www.fighterpilotpodcast.com/author/janek-dev/" /><meta itemprop="name" content="The Fighter Pilot Podcast" /></div><div itemprop="interactionStatistic" itemscope itemtype="https://schema.org/InteractionCounter"><meta itemprop="interactionType" content="https://schema.org/CommentAction" /><meta itemprop="userInteractionCount" content="0" /></div><div class="fl-post-feed-text">
	
		<div class="fl-post-feed-header">

			<h2 class="fl-post-feed-title">
				AARGM
			</h2>

			
			
						<div class="fl-post-feed-meta">
				<div class="fl-post-feed-terms">
					<div class="fl-terms-label"><div class='fl-glossary-cat'><span><span class="armament">Armament</span></span></div></div>
					
			</div>
			
			
		</div>

	
	
	
		
				<div class="fl-post-feed-content">
<p><div id="modal-ready"><p>Advanced Anti-Radiation Guided Missile. A follow-on improvement to the <em><span class="glossary-tooltip glossary-term-5149 glossary-cat-67" tabindex="0"><span class="glossary-link"><span class="glossary-underline">HARM</span></span><span class="hidden glossary-tooltip-content clearfix"><span class="glossary-tooltip-text">High-speed Anti-radiation Missile. A missile designed to home in on surface-to-air radar emitters, such as those affiliated with early warning detection and SAMs.</span></span></span></em>.</p>
</div></p>
		</div>	
	</div>
		</div></div>

<div class="fl-post-grid-post fl-post-align-default post-12916 glossary type-glossary status-publish hentry sort_alphabetical-a glossary-cat-facility-organization wpbf-post" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/CreativeWork">
	<meta itemscope itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage" itemid="https://www.fighterpilotpodcast.com/glossary/aatip/" content="AATIP" /><meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-01-01" /><meta itemprop="dateModified" content="2020-01-24" /><div itemprop="publisher" itemscope itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization"><meta itemprop="name" content="The Fighter Pilot Podcast"><div itemprop="logo" itemscope itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject"><meta itemprop="url" content="https://www.fighterpilotpodcast.com/wp-content/uploads/FPP-Logo-Rgb-Photo-Trademark.png"></div></div><div itemscope itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person"><meta itemprop="url" content="https://www.fighterpilotpodcast.com/author/vincent-host/" /><meta itemprop="name" content="Vincent Aiello" /></div><div itemprop="interactionStatistic" itemscope itemtype="https://schema.org/InteractionCounter"><meta itemprop="interactionType" content="https://schema.org/CommentAction" /><meta itemprop="userInteractionCount" content="0" /></div><div class="fl-post-feed-text">
	
		<div class="fl-post-feed-header">

			<h2 class="fl-post-feed-title">
				AATIP
			</h2>

			
			
						<div class="fl-post-feed-meta">
				<div class="fl-post-feed-terms">
					<div class="fl-terms-label"><div class='fl-glossary-cat'><span><span class="facility-organization">Facility/Organization</span></span></div></div>
					
			</div>
			
			
		</div>

	
	
	
		
				<div class="fl-post-feed-content">
<p><div id="modal-ready"><p>Advanced Aerospace Threat Identification Program. A secret investigatory effort funded by the US Government to study unidentified flying objects.</p>
</div></p>
		</div>	
	</div>
		</div></div>

</div>

		<div class="fl-post-feed-header">

			<h2 class="fl-post-feed-title">
				Ace
			</h2>

			
			
						<div class="fl-post-feed-meta">
				<div class="fl-post-feed-terms">
					<div class="fl-terms-label"><div class='fl-glossary-cat'><span><span class="personnel">Personnel</span></span></div></div>
					
			</div>
			
			
		</div>

	
	
	
		
				<div class="fl-post-feed-content">
<p><div id="modal-ready"><p>A term bestowed on <span class="glossary-tooltip glossary-term-2151 glossary-cat-77" tabindex="0"><span class="glossary-link"><span class="glossary-underline">aircrew</span></span><span class="hidden glossary-tooltip-content clearfix"><span class="glossary-tooltip-text">Generic term for any aircraft crew member, whether at the flight controls or not.</span></span></span> who have downed five or more enemy aircraft in <span class="glossary-tooltip glossary-term-2124 glossary-cat-82" tabindex="0"><span class="glossary-link"><span class="glossary-underline">A/A</span></span><span class="hidden glossary-tooltip-content clearfix"><span class="glossary-tooltip-text">Air-to-air. An aerial fight between two or more aircraft.</span></span></span> combat.</p>
</div></p>
		</div>	
	</div>
		</div></div>

</div>

<div class="fl-post-grid-post fl-post-align-default post-9463 glossary type-glossary status-publish hentry sort_alphabetical-a wpbf-post" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/CreativeWork">
	<meta itemscope itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage" itemid="https://www.fighterpilotpodcast.com/glossary/ace-2/" content="ACE" /><meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-09-21" /><meta itemprop="dateModified" content="2020-01-24" /><div itemprop="publisher" itemscope itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization"><meta itemprop="name" content="The Fighter Pilot Podcast"><div itemprop="logo" itemscope itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject"><meta itemprop="url" content="https://www.fighterpilotpodcast.com/wp-content/uploads/FPP-Logo-Rgb-Photo-Trademark.png"></div></div><div itemscope itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person"><meta itemprop="url" content="https://www.fighterpilotpodcast.com/author/vincent-host/" /><meta itemprop="name" content="Vincent Aiello" /></div><div itemprop="interactionStatistic" itemscope itemtype="https://schema.org/InteractionCounter"><meta itemprop="interactionType" content="https://schema.org/CommentAction" /><meta itemprop="userInteractionCount" content="0" /></div><div class="fl-post-feed-text">
	
		<div class="fl-post-feed-header">

			<h2 class="fl-post-feed-title">
				ACE
			</h2>

			
			
						<div class="fl-post-feed-meta">
				<div class="fl-post-feed-terms">
					<div class="fl-terms-label"></div>
					
			</div>
			
			
		</div>

	
	
	
		
				<div class="fl-post-feed-content">
<p><div id="modal-ready"><p>Aviation Combat Element. A <em><span class="glossary-tooltip glossary-term-9453 glossary-cat-80" tabindex="0"><span class="glossary-link"><span class="glossary-underline">MAGTF</span></span><span class="hidden glossary-tooltip-content clearfix"><span class="glossary-tooltip-text">Marine Air Ground Task Force. A principal United States Marine Corps organization that combines air-, land-, and sea-borne forces to conduct a wide array of military operations and humanitarian responses anywhere in the world. Comprised of a CE, ACE, GCE, and LCE. May take the form of a MEB, MEF, or MEU.</span></span></span></em> component that contributes the force. Includes all aircraft (fixed- and rotary-wing), their pilots and maintenance personnel, and those units necessary for aviation command and control.</p>
</div></p>
		</div>	
	</div>
		</div></div>

</div>

			<h2 class="fl-post-feed-title">
				ACM
			</h2>

			
			
						<div class="fl-post-feed-meta">
				<div class="fl-post-feed-terms">
					<div class="fl-terms-label"></div>
					
			</div>
			
			
		</div>

	
	
	
		
				<div class="fl-post-feed-content">
<p><div id="modal-ready"><p>Air Combat Maneuvering. aka Dogfighting. Close-quarters A/A combat where each pilot tries to shoot down the other, preferably first.</p>
</div></p>
		</div>	
	</div>
		</div></div>

		<div class="fl-post-feed-header">

			<h2 class="fl-post-feed-title">
				ADIZ
			</h2>

			
			
						<div class="fl-post-feed-meta">
				<div class="fl-post-feed-terms">
					<div class="fl-terms-label"></div>
					
			</div>
			
			
		</div>

	
	
	
		
				<div class="fl-post-feed-content">
<p><div id="modal-ready"><p><a href="https://www.faa.gov/air_traffic/publications/us_restrictions/airspace/#adiz" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Air Defense Identification Zone</a>. Airspace over land or water in which the identification, location, and control of civil aircraft is performed in the interest of national security. This airspace may extend beyond a country&#8217;s territory to afford more time to respond to possibly <span class="glossary-tooltip glossary-term-5151 glossary-cat-82" tabindex="0"><span class="glossary-link"><span class="glossary-underline">hostile</span></span><span class="hidden glossary-tooltip-content clearfix"><span class="glossary-tooltip-text">A Bandit for which engagement is authorized.</span></span></span> aircraft.</p>
</div></p>
		</div>	
	</div>
		</div></div>

</div>

				<div class="fl-post-feed-content">

A spring attachment used by the US Navy Blue <span class="glossary-tooltip glossary-term-14384 glossary-cat-82" tabindex="0"><span class="glossary-link"><span class="glossary-underline">Angels</span></span><span class="hidden glossary-tooltip-content clearfix"><span class="glossary-tooltip-text">The height of an aircraft in thousands of feet.</span></span></span> to add tension to the control stick, thus increasing the ability to make small, precise control inputs.</p>

	<meta itemscope itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage" itemid="https://www.fighterpilotpodcast.com/glossary/age/" content="AGE" /><meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-11-12" /><meta itemprop="dateModified" content="2020-01-24" /><div itemprop="publisher" itemscope itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization"><meta itemprop="name" content="The Fighter Pilot Podcast"><div itemprop="logo" itemscope itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject"><meta itemprop="url" content="https://www.fighterpilotpodcast.com/wp-content/uploads/FPP-Logo-Rgb-Photo-Trademark.png"></div></div><div itemscope itemprop="author" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person"><meta itemprop="url" content="https://www.fighterpilotpodcast.com/author/vincent-host/" /><meta itemprop="name" content="Vincent Aiello" /></div><div itemprop="interactionStatistic" itemscope itemtype="https://schema.org/InteractionCounter"><meta itemprop="interactionType" content="https://schema.org/CommentAction" /><meta itemprop="userInteractionCount" content="0" /></div><div class="fl-post-feed-text">
	
		<div class="fl-post-feed-header">

			<h2 class="fl-post-feed-title">
				AGE
			</h2>

			
			
						<div class="fl-post-feed-meta">
				<div class="fl-post-feed-terms">
					<div class="fl-terms-label"><div class='fl-glossary-cat'><span><span class="equipment">Equipment/System</span></span></div></div>
					
			</div>
			
			
		</div>

	
	
	
		
				<div class="fl-post-feed-content">
<p><div id="modal-ready"><p>Aeronautical Ground Equipment. A category of various ground systems used to support military aircraft.  Could include cargo loaders, aircraft tow tractors, and power carts that provide aircraft hydraulic or electrical power or air conditioning for ground operations.</p>
</div></p>
		</div>	
	</div>
		</div></div>

				AGR
			</h2>

			
			
						<div class="fl-post-feed-meta">
				<div class="fl-post-feed-terms">
					<div class="fl-terms-label"><div class='fl-glossary-cat'><span><span class="personnel">Personnel</span></span></div></div>
					
			</div>
			
			
		</div>

	
	
	
		
				<div class="fl-post-feed-content">
<p><div id="modal-ready"><p>Active Guard Reserve. A full-time air national guard reservist. Similar to <em><span class="glossary-tooltip glossary-term-9519 glossary-cat-77" tabindex="0"><span class="glossary-link"><span class="glossary-underline">FTS</span></span><span class="hidden glossary-tooltip-content clearfix"><span class="glossary-tooltip-text">Full Time Support. A US Navy program that allows reservists to perform in positions as full-time active duty members, supporting the Navy Reserve Force.</span></span></span></em>.</p>
</div></p>

<p><div id="modal-ready"><p>Anti-G Straining Maneuver. A technique that employs muscle-tightening and quick breathing in an effort to maintain blood in the cranium when pulling <span class="glossary-tooltip glossary-term-2233" tabindex="0"><span class="glossary-link"><span class="glossary-underline">Gs</span></span><span class="hidden glossary-tooltip-content clearfix"><span class="glossary-tooltip-text">Gravitational Force. The pull of earthâ€™s gravity that people and objects experience as â€œone Gâ€ in an unaccelerated state or â€œzero Gâ€ when falling.</span></span></span>.</p>

var header = jQuery(".sticky-block");
  jQuery(window).scroll(function() {

       if (scroll >= window.innerHeight) {

        } else {

});

<script>
	
    function AdvertisingFade() {
        var divs= jQuery('.advertising-feed .fl-post-feed-post'),
            now = divs.filter(':visible'),
            next = now.next().length ? now.next() : divs.first(),
            speed = 0;
    
        now.fadeOut(speed);
        next.fadeIn(speed);
    }
    
    jQuery(function () {
        setInterval(AdvertisingFade, 10000);
    });

</script>


<script>
  jQuery(document).on("facetwp-refresh", function(){

jQuery.LoadingOverlay("show", {
    image: "",
    progress: true,
		progressClass: "custom-progress-bar",
		background: "none", 
		progressFixedPosition: "bottom"
});
  

    

var count     = 0;
var interval  = setInterval(function(){
    if (count >= 100) {
        clearInterval(interval);
        jQuery.LoadingOverlay("hide");
        return;
    }
    count += 10;
    jQuery.LoadingOverlay("progress", count);
}, 300);
  });
</script>

<script>
jQuery(window).on("load",function() {
  jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
    var windowBottom = jQuery(this).scrollTop() + jQuery(this).innerHeight();
    jQuery("#section-chevron .fl-icon").each(function() {
      /* Check the location of each desired element */
      var objectBottom = jQuery(this).offset().top + 500 + jQuery(this).outerHeight();
      
         if (objectBottom < windowBottom) { 
        if (jQuery(this).css("opacity")==1) {jQuery(this).fadeTo(500,0);}  
        } else { 
        if (jQuery(this).css("opacity")==0) {jQuery(this).fadeTo(500,0);}
      }
    });
  }).scroll(); //invoke scroll-handler on page-load
});

</script>

<script>
jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
 if(jQuery(window).width() <= 1299){
    var fixedBottom = jQuery("#slideout-menu");
    if (jQuery('body').height() <= (jQuery(window).height() + jQuery(window).scrollTop())) {
        fixedBottom.css({'transform': 'translatey(0%)'});
    } else {
        fixedBottom.css({'transform': 'translatey(100%)'});
    }
}
});
</script>







<script>
// hide element after scroll reached section

jQuery(document).ready(function() {
  var topOfOthDiv = jQuery(".home #main");
if (topOfOthDiv.length) {
    var topOfOthDiv = jQuery(".home #main").offset().top;
 jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
    if(jQuery(window).width() > 1300){
        if(jQuery(window).scrollTop() > topOfOthDiv) { //scrolled past the other div?
            jQuery("#slideout-menu").fadeOut(200); //reached the desired point -- show div
        }   else{
  jQuery("#slideout-menu").fadeIn(200);
}
}
});
}
});
</script>





<script>
// open external links in new window
//<![CDATA[
jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
$('p a').each(function() {
var a = new RegExp('/' + window.location.host + '/');
if(!a.test(this.href)) {
$(this).click(function(event) {
event.preventDefault();
event.stopPropagation();
window.open(this.href, '_blank');
});
}
});
});
//]]>
</script>

var osMajorVersion=osVersion.split('.')[0];if(tablet||nexusTablet||iosdevice=='ipad'||(android&&(osMajorVersion==3||(osMajorVersion>=4&&!mobile)))||result.silk){result.tablet=t}else if(mobile||iosdevice=='iphone'||iosdevice=='ipod'||android||nexusMobile||result.blackberry||result.webos||result.bada){result.mobile=t}
if(result.msedge||(result.msie&&result.version>=10)||(result.yandexbrowser&&result.version>=15)||(result.vivaldi&&result.version>=1.0)||(result.chrome&&result.version>=20)||(result.firefox&&result.version>=20.0)||(result.safari&&result.version>=6)||(result.opera&&result.version>=10.0)||(result.ios&&result.osversion&&result.osversion.split(".")[0]>=6)||(result.blackberry&&result.version>=10.1)||(result.chromium&&result.version>=20)){result.a=t;}
else if((result.msie&&result.version<10)||(result.chrome&&result.version<20)||(result.firefox&&result.version<20.0)||(result.safari&&result.version<6)||(result.opera&&result.version<10.0)||(result.ios&&result.osversion&&result.osversion.split(".")[0]<6)||(result.chromium&&result.version<20)){result.c=t}else result.x=t
return result}
var bowser=detect(typeof navigator!=='undefined'?navigator.userAgent:'')
bowser.test=function(browserList){for(var i=0;i<browserList.length;++i){var browserItem=browserList[i];if(typeof browserItem==='string'){if(browserItem in bowser){return true;}}}
return false;}
function getVersionPrecision(version){return version.split(".").length;}
function map(arr,iterator){var result=[],i;if(Array.prototype.map){return Array.prototype.map.call(arr,iterator);}
for(i=0;i<arr.length;i++){result.push(iterator(arr[i]));}
return result;}
function compareVersions(versions){var precision=Math.max(getVersionPrecision(versions[0]),getVersionPrecision(versions[1]));var chunks=map(versions,function(version){var delta=precision-getVersionPrecision(version);version=version+new Array(delta+1).join(".0");return map(version.split("."),function(chunk){return new Array(20-chunk.length).join("0")+chunk;}).reverse();});while(--precision>=0){if(chunks[0][precision]>chunks[1][precision]){return 1;}
else if(chunks[0][precision]===chunks[1][precision]){if(precision===0){return 0;}}
else{return-1;}}}
function isUnsupportedBrowser(minVersions,strictMode,ua){var _bowser=bowser;if(typeof strictMode==='string'){ua=strictMode;strictMode=void(0);}
if(strictMode===void(0)){strictMode=false;}
if(ua){_bowser=detect(ua);}
var version=""+_bowser.version;for(var browser in minVersions){if(minVersions.hasOwnProperty(browser)){if(_bowser[browser]){return compareVersions([version,minVersions[browser]])<0;}}}
return strictMode;}
function check(minVersions,strictMode,ua){return!isUnsupportedBrowser(minVersions,strictMode,ua);}
bowser.isUnsupportedBrowser=isUnsupportedBrowser;bowser.compareVersions=compareVersions;bowser.check=check;bowser._detect=detect;return bowser});(function($){UABBTrigger={triggerHook:function(hook,args)
{$('body').trigger('uabb-trigger.'+hook,args);},addHook:function(hook,callback)
{$('body').on('uabb-trigger.'+hook,callback);},removeHook:function(hook,callback)
{$('body').off('uabb-trigger.'+hook,callback);},};})(jQuery);jQuery(document).ready(function($){if(typeof bowser!=='undefined'&&bowser!==null){var uabb_browser=bowser.name,uabb_browser_v=bowser.version,uabb_browser_class=uabb_browser.replace(/\s+/g,'-').toLowerCase(),uabb_browser_v_class=uabb_browser_class+parseInt(uabb_browser_v);$('html').addClass(uabb_browser_class).addClass(uabb_browser_v_class);}
$('.uabb-row-separator').parents('html').css('overflow-x','hidden');});</script>
